{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"A Colorful Apartment in Moscow With a Parisian Feel","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=432885","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/a-colorful-apartment-in-moscow-with-a-parisian-feel/red-side-moscow-apartment-daria-soboleva-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Red-Side-Moscow-Apartment-Daria-Soboleva-1-810x646.jpg\" alt=\"A Colorful Apartment in Moscow With a Parisian Feel\" /></a></p> \n<p>Measuring 117 square meters, this apartment in Moscow was designed by <a href=\"https://vasilkovadaria.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Daria Vasilkova</a> for a young family with children. France happens to be the travel-loving couple’s favorite country, which led to the designer incorporating a Parisian feel throughout. In addition to the casual French flair, bright colors and contemporary furnishings round out the vibrant design.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432887\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432887\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432887\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Red-Side-Moscow-Apartment-Daria-Soboleva-1m-810x1080.jpg\" 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>The interior incorporates the designer’s own furniture collection, <a href=\"https://vasilkovadaria.com/furniture\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">REDA</a> by Vasilkova Daria, as well as contemporary pieces from Sancal, like the Silencio armchair and ottoman, and Miniforms.</p> eeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/-zgI4nvL_SA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn58@2020_6/2020/10/28/03-03-38-407_c132d903edb82533.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1603854190743},{"createdTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"Find Yourself In the Reflection Collection","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=432645","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/find-yourself-in-the-reflection-collection/reflection-collection-sebastian-errazuriz-sphere-cabinet-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Reflection-Collection-Sebastian-ErraZuriz-Sphere-Cabinet-Featured-Image-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"Find Yourself In the Reflection Collection\" /></a></p> \n<p>It’s only natural to be drawn towards shiny things, but it helps if those things are beautifully designed. <a href=\"https://meetsebastian.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Sebastian Errazuriz’s</a> latest fits the bill on all counts – the Reflection Collection. A new series of handcrafted sculptural <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/furnishings\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">furniture</a> that invites the viewer to look back again and again at the tiny worlds formed inside each prism. There’s no doubt we could all use a look inward for some perspective and introspection, and the depths of each piece of the Reflection Collection mirrors that in theater.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_432727\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432727\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432727\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-432727\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Reflection-Collection-Sebastian-ErraZuriz-Bar-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"bar cabinet\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Reflection-Collection-Sebastian-ErraZuriz-Bar-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Reflection-Collection-Sebastian-ErraZuriz-Bar-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Reflection-Collection-Sebastian-ErraZuriz-Bar-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Reflection-Collection-Sebastian-ErraZuriz-Bar-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Reflection-Collection-Sebastian-ErraZuriz-Bar.jpg 1000w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Bar</p>\n</div> \n<p>“The first piece of the collection was created in memory of my old aunt who told us we could ‘look but never touch’ the beautiful objects she had in her house. The fact that these objects were out of bounds only made them more magical for my brothers and I, who were fascinated at every visit,” explains Errazuriz.</p> \n<p>In a clever twist, the cabinets include an interior light and peepholes that allow the viewer to peek inside and view the objects inside multiplied infinitely like a kaleidoscope. Magical!</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_432728\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432728\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432728\" 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"Globe Partners With PANTONE on Limited-Edition Color of the Year Deck Set","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=432524","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/globe-partners-with-pantone-on-limited-edition-color-of-the-year-deck-set/globe-skateboards-pantone-set1-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-1-810x526.jpg\" alt=\"Globe Partners With PANTONE on Limited-Edition Color of the Year Deck Set\" /></a></p> \n<p>If you’ve followed Design Milk for awhile now, you’re probably aware that we have much appreciation for <a href=\"https://www.pantone.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"> PANTONE </a> and always look forward to announcing the <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/tag/pantone-color-of-the-year/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">PANTONE Color of the Year</a> every December. So, we were pretty thrilled to hear about their latest collaboration. The color experts just partnered with skate brand <a href=\"https://us.globebrand.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Globe</a> on the release of <a href=\"https://us.globebrand.com/products/pantone-coy-box-set-2011-2020?variant=32882696650787\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">two limited edition box sets</a> that include five skate decks, each dipped in a PANTONE Color of the Year from the past 20 years. The 10 colors included in the box sets were carefully considered by the Globe design team, who like many creatives, look to PANTONE for their expertise.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/globe-partners-with-pantone-on-limited-edition-color-of-the-year-deck-set/globe-skateboards-pantone-set1-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432526\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432526\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-2-810x648.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"648\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-2-810x648.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-2-800x640.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-2-768x614.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Each deck, which is a limited edition of 200, is 8.25″ wide x 32″ tall and made from Canadian maple. They are paint dipped in an official PANTONE Color of the Year and then engraved with the color name and PANTONE number on the top. Then they are laser-etched with information about the color and collaboration, as well as the individualized number of the edition on each top.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/globe-partners-with-pantone-on-limited-edition-color-of-the-year-deck-set/globe-skateboards-pantone-set1-3/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432527\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432527\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-3-810x1013.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1013\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-3-810x1013.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-3-800x1000.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-3-768x960.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-3-1229x1536.jpg 1229w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Globe-Skateboards-Pantone-Set1-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>The <a href=\"https://us.globebrand.com/products/pantone-coy-box-set-2011-2020?variant=32882696650787\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">1st box set</a>, which recently launched, features Color of the Year picks from 2011 – 2020, which results in a vivid color palette:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>2020 Classic Blue PANTONE 19-4052</li> \n <li>2019 Living Coral PANTONE 16-1546</li> \n <li>2018 Ultra Violet PANTONE 18-3838</li> \n <li>2017 Greenery PANTONE 15-0343</li> \n <li>2012 Tangerine Tango PANTONE 17-1463</li> \n</ul> \n<p>The 2nd box set, which is set to be released on November 6th, offers a warmer, more muted tone palette with Color of the Year selections from 2000 – 2010:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>2010 Turquoise PANTONE 15-5519</li> \n <li>2009 Mimosa PANTONE 14-0848</li> \n <li>2006 Sand Dollar PANTONE 13-1106</li> \n <li>2002 True Red PANTONE 19-1664</li> \n <li>2000 Cerulean Blue PANTONE 15-4020</li> \n</ul> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/globe-partners-with-pantone-on-limited-edition-color-of-the-year-deck-set/globe-skateboards-pantone-set1-5/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432529\" 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"A Dental Office in Paris That Feels More Like Home","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=432660","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/a-dental-office-in-paris-that-feels-more-like-home/le-berre-vevaud-dental-clinic-paris-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Le-Berre-Vevaud-Dental-Clinic-Paris-1-810x607.jpg\" alt=\"A Dental Office in Paris That Feels More Like Home\" /></a></p> \n<p>Dental offices around the globe should take note of the <a href=\"https://leberrevevaud.com/project/georges-mandel\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">latest project</a> by interior designers Raphaël Le Berre and Thomas Vevaud of <a href=\"https://leberrevevaud.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Le Berre Vevaud</a>. They transformed a former Haussmann-style apartment in Paris into a modern dental clinic with a delightful color palette and furnishings that give it a cozy and inviting atmosphere – an atmosphere far better than any dental clinic I’ve ever seen.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432662\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432662\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Le-Berre-Vevaud-Dental-Clinic-Paris-1m-768x1152.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432663\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432663\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432663\" https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Le-Berre-Vevaud-Dental-Clinic-Paris-2-768x1025.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432664\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432664\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432664\" pink, nudes, blues and mustard for a warm yet vibrant aesthetic that’s bound to make anyone’s appointment a more relaxed one. You might even forget you’re at the dentist!</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432665\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432665\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432665\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Le-Berre-Vevaud-Dental-Clinic-Paris-3.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1081\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Le-Berre-Vevaud-Dental-Clinic-Paris-3.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Le-Berre-Vevaud-Dental-Clinic-Paris-3-800x1068.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Le-Berre-Vevaud-Dental-Clinic-Paris-3-768x1025.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>In the waiting room, there’s a vintage sofa, a blue/green Chinoz lamp from Parachilna, and a hanging Arrangements fixture by Michael Anastassiades for Flos. The rest of the furnishings are custom pieces made by Le Berre Vevaud, including the rug produced by Taiping, the coffee table and console.</p> \n<p><a dn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn18@2020_2/2020/10/28/03-03-35-024_b5477885be06c803.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Le-Berre-Vevaud-Dental-Clinic-Paris-30.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn3@2020_2/2020/10/28/03-03-35-029_4b898c95d3ae1078.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/ZAWp5zS0Ms4":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn9@2020_3/2020/10/28/03-03-39-771_4681e3bae9b63a75.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1603854190758},{"createdTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"Jacqueline de la Fuente Turns Waste Paper + Cardboard Into Sculptural Vases","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=432860","description":"<p><em><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/tag/Circular-by-Design/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Circular by Design</a>, a fortnightly column by longtime contributor <a href=\"https://katietreggiden.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Katie Treggiden</a>, explores the reuse of waste as a way to keep materials in use and bring the legacy of the linear system full circle.</em></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/jacqueline-de-la-fuente-turns-waste-paper-cardboard-into-sculptural-vases/de_la_jardin_design_milk_00/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_00-810x355.jpg\" alt=\"Jacqueline de la Fuente Turns Waste Paper + Cardboard Into Sculptural Vases\" /></a></p> \n<p>UK-based artist and designer Jacqueline de la Fuente was inspired to start making sculptural vases from waste paper and cardboard when she had children – from noticing the increase in waste her family now generated, through experimenting with papier-mâché alongside them, and through wanting to leave them the legacy of a healthier planet on which to grow up. Through her studio, <a href=\"http://www.delajardin.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">De La Jardin</a>, she now hand-makes eye-catching decorative objects which are sought-after by interior designers and private collectors alike. We spoke to Jacqueline to find out more.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_432869\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432869\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432869\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"wp-image-432869 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_05-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_05-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_05-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_05-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_05-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_05-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_05.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Jacqueline de la Fuente</p>\n</div> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432873\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432873\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432873\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_01-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_01-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_01-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_01-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_01-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_01-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_01.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>Tell me a little bit about your childhood, education and background in terms of how you first became interested in creativity, design and sustainability.</strong></p> \n<p>I was born in England, Surrey but my parents are both from the Philippines and came over to study nursing in the 1970s. When I was eight years old my parents decided to move us to the Philippines where we lived for two years. Growing up I preferred being outdoors than drawing, but discovered my creative streak when it came to my art lessons – I was always doing more than was asked, pushing the boundaries, but not really noticing it at the time. Having lived in both countries I was aware of how different they were from a young age. We lived comfortably in both places, but in the Philippines, I was much more aware of the pollution and how the poorer areas suffered environmentally. I guess this has subconsciously stuck with me. Moving back to the UK, I went on to pursue interior design on a foundation course but without any planning, I fell into textile design. I went onto Winchester School of Art where I specialized in weave design – again without any real planning! This gave me an understanding of how fabric was made and the labour involved. After graduating I decided to travel to Australia where I ended up working as a weave and print designer. I then travelled to the weaving mills in China, and that was a definite moment where I became aware of the impact the textile industry was having on the environment – how the dyes were disposed of and the process the yarns would go through.</p> \n<p><strong>How would you describe your work? </strong></p> \n<p>My work is designed to turn discarded unwanted paper into artful decorative, ornamental pieces for people to enjoy and have in their home. My vases and sculptures are hand-sculpted, using paper and card waste which is turned into a paper clay. Each vase or sculpture I make is a piece of art to be treasured. At the same time, they have an organic feel to them with the combination of structure and boldness.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432868\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432868\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432868\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_06-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_06-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_06-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_06-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_06-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_06-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_06.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What inspired this project?</strong></p> \n<p>My passion for ceramics, objects, sculptures and vases initially inspired this project. Being a full-time mum to two young kids meant going to a ceramics studio wasn’t easily accessible for me. At the same time, having a family made me aware of how much we throw away such as packaging of kids’ toys, cereal boxes, letters, egg cartons… One day after researching papier-mâché for my kids, I came across a lady who was making theatre props out of ‘paper clay’. Her version was more like a soft paste that you had to use over chicken wire for structure and she was using tissue instead of paper. This instantly clicked with me and inspired me to think about how I could use our paper and card waste and turn it into clay. It dawned on me just how very little we pay attention to these materials and I was curious to see if I could prolong their use by changing their form and aesthetic.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432871\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432871\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432871\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_03-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_03-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_03-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_03-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_03-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_03-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_03.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What waste (and other) materials are you using, how did you select those particular materials and how do you source them?</strong></p> \n<p>I source paper and card waste from local cafes, shops and what we throw away in our own home. This is from packaging, letters, newspapers, egg cartons – all of which are discarded almost instantly after their short use. To make the clay, I turn these into paper pulp and mix them with flour, adhesive and a small amount of joint compound so very similar to papier-mâché. I like the idea that these materials go through less of a process than normal recycling. Very little energy apart from my own is used to turn waste paper into a new aesthetic.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432870\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432870\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432870\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_04-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_04-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_04-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_04-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_04-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_04-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_04.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>When did you first become interested in using waste as raw material and what motivated this decision? </strong></p> \n<p>As much as working in the design industry made me aware of the materials we use and the processes that create waste, it is becoming a mum that has given me the motivation. From food waste to items the kids grow out off or no longer want to play with, the realization of just how much we end up taking to the charity shops, selling on eBay or throwing away became overwhelming and I felt I had to do something about it.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432872\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432872\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432872\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_02-810x915.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"915\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_02-810x915.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_02-800x904.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_02-768x868.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_02.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What processes do the materials have to undergo to become the finished product? </strong></p> \n<p>To make the paper clay, I first shred the card and paper by hand. This is then soaked in water until it’s softened enough to blend it, turning into paper pulp. To hold the paper pulp together, I mix in a small amount of adhesive, joint compound and flour to the pulp which makes it into a sturdier malleable clay. The process uses very little water and hardly any clay goes to waste. I can pretty much start making it into a shape straight away. Unlike normal clay, each part of the object needs to be made individually as it’s still quite soft. I sometimes use glass jars or recycled objects I have at home to help start off a shape or base and then use my hands to organically build up the desired shape I have in mind. By adapting the recipe and using paper and card instead of tissue for the clay, it makes it more malleable and easier to mold into shape. Some of my vases are left naturally or I paint them with water-based paint which are from sustainable companies.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432867\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432867\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432867\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_07-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_07-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_07-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_07-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_07-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_07-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_07.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What happens to your products at the end of their life – can they go back into the circular economy? </strong></p> \n<p>If I’m honest my vases have not got to the stage yet of being discarded so I don’t know how well they break down. As they are not watertight, I am sure that by wetting them again, the material would turn back into clay but it won’t go back to its original material or paper again.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432866\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432866\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432866\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_08-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_08-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_08-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_08-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_08-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_08-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_08.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>How did you feel the first time you saw the transformation from waste material to product/prototype?</strong></p> \n<p>Seeing the vases I made for the first time was very exciting and I was amazed that I had created a product that was very similar to ceramics in terms of how it looks and feels in the hand.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432864\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432864\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432864\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_09-810x961.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"961\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_09-810x961.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_09-800x949.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_09-768x911.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_09.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>How have people reacted to this project?</strong></p> \n<p>When I first made my vases it took a while for me to share them as I was hesitant about whether people would understand why I was using paper and card waste to make decorative objects for interiors and home – I was also worried that the materials I was using would cheapen them, even though the craftsmanship is the same when working with hand-building clay. The moment I shared them on social media, I had the most amazing response. The first (and only!) three vases I had made sold instantly and from there I started getting orders and interest from all sorts of people even the amazing interior design duo <a href=\"http://www.2lgstudio.com/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">2LG Studio</a>. I now have a great following and lots of interest in the process of how I make the final product. People seem to be excited to have my vases or sculptures in their home or to give them to family or friends as gifts.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432862\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432862\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432862\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_11-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_11-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_11-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_11-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_11-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_11-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_11.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>How do you feel opinions towards waste as a raw material are changing?</strong></p> \n<p>People are more aware of sustainability, buying or sourcing locally to cut down their carbon footprints. With our current situation with climate change and COVID-19, I think people are becoming more aware of waste and reusing what they can, buying less and making more considered purchases. By looking at how things are made and materials, people are more positive and accepting towards waste being used in products or as a new material.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432863\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432863\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432863\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_10-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_10-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_10-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_10-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_10-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_10-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_10.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What do you think the future holds for waste as a raw material?</strong></p> \n<p>As our resources dwindle and people become more aware of waste and the impact on the environment, recycling discarded waste into innovative materials is the way forward. We can see it now in the various creative industries that are beginning to do this, for example, plastic bottles made into handbags or into tables and chairs. They are so many exciting new products out there made purely from recycled waste. I hope this can continue in other areas.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://katietreggiden.com/designmilk/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img src=\"https://katietreggiden.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Custom-650x300-Design-Milk-2020.gif\" alt=\"advertisement for wasted by katie treggiden\" width=\"650\" height=\"300\" /></a></p> \n<img -126_79d2c62f098e5df2.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/De_La_Jardin_Design_Milk_10-810x810.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn30@2020_6/2020/10/28/03-03-35-242_a0df2a9741310153.webp","https://katietreggiden.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Custom-650x300-Design-Milk-2020.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn24@2020_5/2020/10/28/03-03-36-095_4b374a3338454e2d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/niV58vkgd3w":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn67@2020_3/2020/10/28/03-03-34-995_0922a4e8e327a9bc.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1603854190747},{"createdTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"Bang and Olufsen’s New Remote Operates Under a Halo Effect","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=429956","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/bang-and-olufsens-new-remote-operates-under-a-halo-effect/bo_beoremote_halo-3/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/BO_Beoremote_Halo-3-810x621.jpg\" alt=\"Bang and Olufsen’s New Remote Operates Under a Halo Effect\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/bang-olufsen\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Bang and Olufsen’s</a> latest home audio device, the <a href=\"https://www.bang-olufsen.com/en/accessories/beoremote-halo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Beoremote Halo</a>, is a bit of an unexpected throwback – at least functionally – an aluminum ring-shaped console system reintroducing the tactile connection between music and listener in a singular control device, harkening to a pre-app/network audio-era when home audio systems relied solely upon physical remote controls.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=429959\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-429959\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-429959\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/BO_Beoremote_Halo-2-810x964.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"964\" /></a></p> \n<p>The Danish audio brand is renown for their <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/bang-olufsen\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">sculptural interpretations of home audio</a> intended to flex visually as much as aurally, and they don’t disappoint in this department with a design piece intended to be as much fashionable as functional, free-standing device or wall mounted.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=429965\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-429965\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-429965\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/LS_07.2020_Halo_Alu_Wall.tif-810x682.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"682\" /></a></p> \n<p>The Beoremote Halo’s main function beyond looking oh-so-nice is to connect and control any of the brand’s high-end Beolab speakers – including the Beolab 90, Beolab 50, Beolab 1 8, Beosound Shape – alongside any of their more affordable multi-room speakers the Danish brand offers. The system displays current song, lists all connected devices and allows the customization of additional output settings.</p> \n<section class=\"shop-inline-featured-products\"> \n <div class=\"section-heading clearfix\"> \n  <img style=\"width: auto;\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/img/dashed-lines-white.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"dashed-lines\" /> \n  <h3>From The Shop</h3> \n </div> \n <div class=\"shop-inline-featured-products-inner\"> \n  <div class=\"shop-inline-product-left\"> \n   <div class=\"article-list-item\"> \n    <a style=\"text-decoration: none;\" href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/products/anthracite-bang-olufsen-beoplay-a9-4th-generation-with-voice-assist-wireless-multiroom-speaker?utm_source=shop_module_post_interstitial_shoppable_product\" class=\"article-image hover-image product-article-image has-standard-product-image\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"> <img src=\"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0250/0322/9287/products/bang-olufsen-speakers-anthracite-beoplay-a9-4th-gen-voice-assist-wireless-multiroom-speaker-design-milk-shop-14174593744999.jpg?v=1597195154\" style=\"width: 100%;\" alt=\"Anthracite Beoplay A9 4th Gen + Voice Assist Wireless Multiroom Speaker\" /> \n     <div class=\"category-label\">\n      <span class=\"label-text\">Shop</span>\n      <span class=\"ss-right ss-standard\"></span>\n     </div> </a> \n    <div class=\"article-content\"> \n     <h3><a style=\"color: black; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen=\"\"></iframe></p> \n<p>The Beoremote turns on automatically when approached, offering users a bit of that satisfying haptic feedback while adjusting the volume swiping across its solid aluminum ring surface with the ability to start or stop listening to music with a single button press. The video above from a Bang and Olufsen British dealer shows the control system in action.</p> \n<section class=\"shop-inline-featured-products\"> \n <div class=\"section-heading clearfix\"> \n  <img 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"Heymat Releases Foliage Mat Collection Inspired by Mother Earth","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=432937","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/heymat-releases-foliage-mat-collection-inspired-by-mother-earth/heymat-foliage-mat-kristine-five-melvaer-1-blue/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HeyMat-Foliage-Mat-Kristine-Five-Melvaer-1-blue-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"Heymat Releases Foliage Mat Collection Inspired by Mother Earth\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/heymat\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Heymat</a> has been on <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/heymat-brings-modern-design-doorstep/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">our radar</a> for a few years now with their floor mats that merge the high quality of industrial mats with Scandinavian design. The Norwegian brand’s latest collection, Foliage designed by Oslo-based designer <a href=\"https://www.heymat.com/designer/kristine-five-melvaer/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Kristine Five Melvær</a>, lets you bring a bit of nature into your home via three colorways and a pattern inspired by Mother Earth.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/heymat-releases-foliage-mat-collection-inspired-by-mother-earth/heymat-foliage-mat-kristine-five-melvaer-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432939\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432939\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HeyMat-Foliage-Mat-Kristine-Five-Melvaer-2-810x1206.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1206\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HeyMat-Foliage-Mat-Kristine-Five-Melvaer-2-810x1206.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HeyMat-Foliage-Mat-Kristine-Five-Melvaer-2-800x1191.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HeyMat-Foliage-Mat-Kristine-Five-Melvaer-2-768x1144.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HeyMat-Foliage-Mat-Kristine-Five-Melvaer-2-1032x1536.jpg 1032w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HeyMat-Foliage-Mat-Kristine-Five-Melvaer-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Since their launch in 2015, <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/heymat\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Heymat</a> has worked to make the products and their production process as sustainable and environmentally friendly as possible. In 2017 they moved to a new material from 50% recycled plastic that offered a better absorption capacity. And beginning Autumn 2020, they’re made with a 100% recycled plastic (PET) textile. Depending on the size, one Heymat now reuses 33-82 plastic bottles (.5 liter)! The mats come with an anti-slip backing in nitrile rubber to ensure they stay right where they’re placed. When it’s time for a cleaning, you can either vacuum them or throw them in a domestic washing machine at 140°F.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/heymat-releases-foliage-mat-collection-inspired-by-mother-earth/heymat-foliage-mat-kristine-five-melvaer-3/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432940\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-432940 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HeyMat-Foliage-Mat-Kristine-Five-Melvaer-3-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"\" 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Foliage mats are available in a 60cm x 85cm (24in x 33in) size and a 85cm x 115cm (33in x 45in) size, and come in <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/heymat/products/foliage-mat-green-dawn-1\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Green Dawn</a>.</p> \n<p><a da001b0c0b.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1603854190755},{"createdTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"The Nailed Sculpture of Robert Kobayashi","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=431844","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/the-nailed-sculpture-of-robert-kobayashi/robertkobayashi_susaninglett_01/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_01-810x601.jpg\" alt=\"The Nailed Sculpture of Robert Kobayashi\" /></a></p> \n<p>Robert Kobayashi’s <a href=\"https://www.inglettgallery.com/exhibitions/robert-kobayashi-moe-s-meat-market\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">intensely nailed sculptures</a> are a textural treat for the eyes. Each object radiates the inspiring spirit of an artist who blazed his own path to eventually find his home (and personal art gallery) in a former butcher shop in Little Italy. <a href=\"https://www.inglettgallery.com/exhibitions/robert-kobayashi-moe-s-meat-market\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">“Moe’s Meat Market”</a>, a selection of sculpture and a documentation of his unusual art space, is on view at <a href=\"https://www.inglettgallery.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Susan Inglett Gallery</a> in New York through November 7<sup>th</sup>.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_431846\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431846\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431846\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431846\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_02-810x759.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"759\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_02-810x759.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_02-800x749.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_02-768x719.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_02.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Glass Cup, 1998</p>\n</div> \n<p>Kobayashi (1925-2015) used thin metal strips cut from metal he found in Little Italy (old ceiling tin, Café Bustelo coffee cans, beer cans and more) that he painted, and nailed to wood supports. The sculptures echo the neighborhood itself – perhaps the flower arrangements at nearby sidewalk flower shop – and also prove a great love of Art History.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_431847\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431847\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431847\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431847\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_03-810x681.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"681\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_03-810x681.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_03-800x673.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_03-768x646.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_03.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Still Life in the 1930’s, 1997</p>\n</div> \n<div id=\"attachment_431848\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431848\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431848\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431848\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_04-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_04-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_04-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_04-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_04.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Still Life in the 1930’s, 1997 (detail)</p>\n</div> \n<div id=\"attachment_431849\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431849\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431849\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431849\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_05-810x768.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"768\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_05-810x768.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_05-800x758.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_05-768x728.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_05.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Flowers Seeking Attention, 2002</p>\n</div> \n<p>Robert Kobayashi was born in 1925 in Honolulu and served in the military during World War II. After studying at the Honolulu Academy of Art, he moved to NYC in 1950 to attend the Brooklyn Museum School of Art and was soon hired by MoMA to tend to a Japanese house and garden. He stayed on staff for more than two decades and was a regular in the gallery world – showcasing his work at 25 solo exhibitions and countless group exhibitions. In short, Kobayashi was tightly connected and involved in the art world, which is what makes his move to his own “gallery” inside a former butcher shop – and outside the typical “gallery neighborhood” – so intriguing and inspiring.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_431857\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431857\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431857\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431857\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_13-810x536.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"536\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_13-810x536.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_13-800x529.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_13-768x508.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_13.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Kobi, His Daugher Misa, and Janice Parente during “Red Curtain”, 1990, by Kate Keller Kobayashi</p>\n</div> \n<p>He purchased the former butcher shop at 237 Elizabeth Street in Little Italy in 1977 with his wife, the photographer Kate Keller Kobayashi where they lived and created art. Susan Inglett Gallery has complied a fantastic <a href=\"https://en.calameo.com/read/006031000c36771b75495\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">digital catalog</a> with more photographs and personal stories told by his wife (click to the back of the e-book) that is well worth a click-through.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_431856\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431856\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431856\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431856\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_12-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_12-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_12-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_12-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_12.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Wild Flowers Gathered Along Route 80, 2009 (detail)</p>\n</div> \n<div id=\"attachment_431855\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431855\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431855\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431855\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_11-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_11-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_11-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_11-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_11.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Robert Kobayashi: Moe’s Meat Market. Installation at Susan Inglett Gallery, 2020</p>\n</div> \n<p>This 2020 re-introduction of his life and work includes a small back room with a facsimile of the original tile floors and various joyful photographs through the decades of his space. We dare you not to smile.</p> \n<p>Kobayashi’s story would be a great movie, but his actual artwork is even more magnetic. The hundreds of nails go far beyond their “function” to give an energetic visual sparkle. You can almost hear the tapping with your eyes. </p> \n<p>For the subject matter – in addition to the neighborhood references and whimsical nods to art history in several “nudes” and still lifes, there are a number of very clever visual plays. The glass bottles for example, are defined only by a ghostly cut outline but punctuated with a deep black shadow.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_431851\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431851\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431851\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431851\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_07-810x687.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"687\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_07-810x687.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_07-800x678.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_07-768x651.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_07.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Eastern Standard Time, Vermont, 2001</p>\n</div> \n<div id=\"attachment_431850\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431850\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431850\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431850\" 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">White on White, 2012 (detail)</p>\n</div> \n<p>The original location of “Moe’s Meat Market” closed in 2017, two years after his death at the age of 90. You should not miss your chance to see THIS exhibition in person.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_431854\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431854\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431854\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431854\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_10-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_10-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_10-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_10-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/RobertKobayashi_SusanInglett_10.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Robert Kobayashi: Moe’s Meat Market. 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"Easy Peasy Lighting Welcomes a New Era at Lodes","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=432745","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/easy-peasy-lighting-welcomes-a-new-era-at-lodes/easy-peasy-table-lamp-lodes-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-Featured-Image-810x472.jpg\" alt=\"Easy Peasy Lighting Welcomes a New Era at Lodes\" /></a></p> \n<p>Rebranding from Studio Italia Design to <a href=\"https://www.lodes.com/?lang=en\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Lodes</a> in June, the <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/lighting\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">lighting</a> company is also celebrating their 70th anniversary with a refreshed approach to innovation and contemporary design. One of the first pieces introduced under this new design mindset is the <a href=\"https://www.lodes.com/prodotto/easy-peasy/?lang=en\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Easy Peasy</a> table lamp by <a href=\"http://nichettostudio.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Luca Nichetto</a>. Sculptural in form with a shape reminiscent of a bell, the Easy Peasy collection consists of four portable and rechargeable table lamps.</p> \n<div> \n <p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432750\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432750\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432750\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-1-810x360.jpg\" alt=\"group of lamps\" width=\"810\" height=\"360\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-1-810x360.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-1-800x356.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-1-768x342.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-1.jpg 1000w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n <p>Featuring a metal base housing the LED light source and diffuser, a glass body, and a solid plastic rounded knob, Easy Peasy is materially diverse. The knob is used to turn the lamp on and off, as well as to control the dimmer. A micro-USB socket at the base enables users to recharge the lamp’s battery.</p> \n <p>Choose from four stunning color combinations that have been inspired by nature: Flamingo, Lagoon, Kelp or Chestnut.</p> \n <p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432751\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432751\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432751\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-2-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"lamps closeup\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-2-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-2-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-2-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Easy-Peasy-Table-Lamp-LODES-2.jpg 1000w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n <p>Luca Nichetto, designer of Easy Peasy as well as Design Curator of Lodes, adds, “The products we are launching emphasize this need to further expand on the relationship between products and users by blending form and function. Today’s design requires a seamless integration of interaction and technological performance to create pieces that not only are aesthetically pleasing, but also serve a function and create a connection.”</p> \n <p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=432752\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-432752\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432752\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Blueair-Blue-Auto-810x551.jpg\" alt=\"Blueair Blue Pure Auto Find Inspiration in the Scandinavian Landscape\" /></a></p> \n<p>Air quality has entered into the forefront of many people’s minds lately. And while we cannot always control the quality of air outside, air purification indoors is something all households can improve almost immediately with the introduction of an efficient HEPA-grade air purifier. Blueair’s latest line of <a href=\"https://www.blueair.com/us/blue\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Blue Pure Auto Air Purifiers</a> improve on their highly rated performance with the addition of several notable upgrades, including an aesthetic addition of five optional washable pre-filter colors inspired by the natural landscapes of Scandinavia.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/blueair-blue-air-purifiers-scandinavian-landscape/blueauto_411_lineup/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431870\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-431870\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_lineup-810x389.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"389\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_lineup-810x389.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_lineup-800x384.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_lineup-768x369.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_lineup.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>The Swedish air quality appliance brand’s air filtering solutions – particularly their Blue line – soften the presence of what can be an intrusive presence within interior spaces with the combination of simple cylindrical or square designs covered with pre-filter fabrics. The newly updated line of Blue Pure Auto air purifiers now can be customized with five optional washable pre-filters in hues derived from the Scandinavian natural landscape (Arctic Trail, a gray color cover is included).</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/blueair-blue-air-purifiers-scandinavian-landscape/pre-filter/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431869\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-431869\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Pre-Filter-810x428.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"428\" id=\"attachment_431868\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/blueair-blue-air-purifiers-scandinavian-landscape/blueauto_411_pdp_feature2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431868\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"wp-image-431868 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_pdp_feature2-810x657.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"657\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_pdp_feature2-810x657.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_pdp_feature2-800x649.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_pdp_feature2-768x623.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/blueauto_411_pdp_feature2.jpg 1000w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Blue Pure Auto Air Purifiers use a combination of a particle filter and carbon filter made from natural coconut carbon to remove 99.97% of airborne particles and household odors.</p>\n</div> \n<p>Their bona fides in the air filtration department have been <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/wirecutter/reviews/best-air-purifier/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">proven in independent testing</a>, and these new designs now include an integrated LED Air Quality Indicator and one-touch Auto mode feature that increases fan speed when the particle sensor determines interior air quality has dropped. A lower and quieter speed returns once pollution dissipates, simplifying the introduction of air purification at home. Thankfully each model is also designed with an auto-dimming light, reducing the annoyance of device light pollution.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_431871\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/blueair-blue-air-purifiers-scandinavian-landscape/blue_extension_medium_hero_high_transparent/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431871\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"wp-image-431871 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Blue_Extension_Medium_Hero_High_Transparent-810x659.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"659\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Blue_Extension_Medium_Hero_High_Transparent-810x659.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Blue_Extension_Medium_Hero_High_Transparent-800x651.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Blue_Extension_Medium_Hero_High_Transparent-768x625.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Blue_Extension_Medium_Hero_High_Transparent.jpg 1200w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">The Blue Pure Auto Air Purifiers line have a somewhat confusing numerical naming scheme where the higher the model number, the smaller the coverage of filtration. The 411 Auto ($119.99) is designed for smaller spaces like a nursery, guest bedroom or home office and can filter up to 190 ft². The 311 Auto ($239.99) is designed for bedrooms and living rooms of up to 388 ft², while the largest 211+ Auto ($299) can handle rooms as large as 540 ft².</p>\n</div> \n<img 11:03:10","updatedTime":"2020-10-28 11:03:10","title":"HP DesignJet Studio Printer Blends Into Any Workspace","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=431733","description":"<p><em>The following post is brought to you by <a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">HP</a>. Our partners are hand picked by the Design Milk team because they represent the best in design.</em></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/hp-designjet-studio-printer-blends-into-any-workspace/hp-designjet-3/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-3-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"HP DesignJet Studio Printer Blends Into Any Workspace\" /></a></p> \n<p>If there’s one thing 2020 will leave upon us moving forward, it will be the imprint of months of working from home. The new paradigm related to workflow, tools and collaborative adaptations within creative teams have all redefined the “workspace.” Going to work now is not so much of a place as it is a mindset. Almost anywhere can become a workspace as long as the right tools remain accessible. With work continuing to migrate toward a home-centered reality for the foreseeable future, companies like HP are pivoting toward solutions like the new <a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">DesignJet Studio</a> series large-format plotters, purposely designed to blend into workflows within both traditional creative studio spaces or shared amongst team members remotely.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_432261\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"wp-image-432261 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-workshop-bussines-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-workshop-bussines-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-workshop-bussines-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-workshop-bussines-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-workshop-bussines-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-workshop-bussines.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">The DesignJet Studio’s compact furniture-like footprint is designed to elegantly reduce the distracting visual clutter typically introduced with the presence of a large format printer.</p>\n</div> \n<p>The mere presence of a large device like a plotter printer tends to become a visual pain point within a studio. They’re generally hidden away with the likes of the copy machine in an office. But where do you put it in a home environment, where our work devices need to share space with our personal lives?</p> \n<p>Thus HP took on a more holistic approach to their proven printing technology. “Furniture that prints” – a guiding ethos resulting in a plotter equipped with details that takes cues from the realm of interior decor: a warmly finished wood veneer roll cover, lightweight contemporary wired frame legs, an integrated bin resembling a magazine rack. Compare this to the traditional design of plotters of yore – enormous industrial-style pieces of hardware balancing upon a set of hefty legs – and it becomes obvious the lightweight presence of the <a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">DesignJet Studio</a>‘s is an aesthetic epiphany, especially in its smaller and home office-friendly <a href=\"https://bit.ly/2J7aMou\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">24″ iteration</a>.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432251\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Close_up-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Close_up-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Close_up-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Close_up-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Close_up-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Close_up.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<blockquote>\n <p>“When considering color, materiality and finish for our design, our inspiration came from the beautiful small studios and home studios of architects and designers where our device is intended to blend into. We researched these types of work spaces, the most common materials used and the style of furniture and décor that typically outfit these environments. Through our ´furniture that prints´ ethos, our goal was to create a calm tech solution that is only there when you need it.” – Joey Zeledon, Head of Industrial Design, HP Barcelona</p>\n</blockquote> \n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-432250\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Process-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Process-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Process-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Process-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Process-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio_Process.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-431735\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-2-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-2-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-2-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-2-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-2-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>HP also emphasizes the ability to empower remote teamwork with a mobile device solution. <a href=\"https://bit.ly/3muzMVb\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">HP Mobile Printing</a> is an app-based tool designed to simplify printing, scanning and the sharing of documents via smartphone or tablet. The Android and iOS compatible app also gives users the ability to access and automate projects easily, even if the user is hundreds of miles away.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_432262\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"wp-image-432262 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-greta-hp-click_b-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-greta-hp-click_b-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-greta-hp-click_b-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-greta-hp-click_b-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-greta-hp-click_b-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP_DesignJet_Studio-greta-hp-click_b.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Whether working at home or in a shared space, the DesignJet Studio’s remote sharing tools empower users to work collaboratively.</p>\n</div> \n<p>While a great deal of attention was placed upon the industrial design at a surface level, the plotter’s appeal isn’t meant to be merely skin deep. The HP DesignJet Studio is also the company’s first net carbon neutral plotter, spearheading an initiative to reduce the carbon footprint associated with printing at large format sizes. HP improved the energy efficiency of the HP DesignJet Studio, while also reducing the amount of packaging attached to shipping the device and integrating the use of recycled plastics in the manufacturing process.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_431736\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://bit.ly/3kvt1lp\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\"><img class=\"wp-image-431736 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-1-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-1-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-1-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-1-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-1-600x337.jpg 600w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/HP-DesignJet-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">The HP DesignJet Studio <a href=\"https://bit.ly/31FEB5J\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">is available in 24” and 36” output sizes</a>, with the option for a wood veneer and steel finish available for both.</p>\n</div> \n<p>Lastly, HP has taken great efforts to reduce a major friction point traditionally attached to printer plotters intended for professional settings: setup. Emphasizing simplicity, the DesignJet Studio arrives with HP’s first mobile onboarding experience, replacing confusingly long instructions with an easy-to-follow guided setup encompassing features of the printer, mobile iOS or Android app and desktop integration – in sum, a printer allowing users to focus energies upon the creative rather than fuss with the technical.</p> \n<p><iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/-8EbzcGzOLs\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p> \n<img Topped with an alpaca pad, the round seats rest upon oak legs hidden by layered discs of leather, the same design detail found on the seat backs. Two columns rise up from the seat to connect the blown glass tubes filled with helium glass, which emit a soft neon glow.
